Iris' eyes widened for a moment at the sudden confession.

"...Fan?"

Fariel looked down, but continued with serious eyes.

``I read the report on the destruction of Zima Oil alone.
Also the battle log for capturing Leon...
In that situation, calmly and gracefully overwhelming the enemy...
I really respect you!
I can't believe Vermilion has such an amazing person at the top...
I'm proud! ”

Iris laughed a little shyly,
He lightly brushed off his white haori.

“Thank you, Fariel.
But we're still halfway through.
"Silver Venom harbors a deeper darkness."

Miyushari happily poked Fariel with her elbow,
I changed the topic.

"By the way, about Fiona.
That person is the COO of Fallujah in Miertenga territory, right?
　The actual number 2 among large international companies is
I can't believe he went all the way to Blue Rose to rescue Vivietta.
　You're not just an ordinary person after all.

In my personal opinion, I think Fiona is the ultimate "corporate warrior".
Although she is outwardly a businesswoman,
Behind the scenes, he is acting on his own beliefs.
Using the power of Fallujah,
I think they're keeping an eye on organizations like Silver Venom.''

Iris nodded silently.

“...That’s right.
I heard that Fiona has already returned to Miertenga.
Vivietta is resting at Blue Rose.
I'm glad both of you are safe."

Miyushari smiled,
I clenched my fist lightly.

"Then it's our turn to get serious.
Director Iris, let's uncover the darkness of Silver Venom together!
Fariel is also excited as a fan, right? ”

Fariel blushed,
I nodded vigorously.

"...Yes! It's an honor to fight alongside Chief Iris!"

Iris saw their enthusiasm,
I smiled quietly but surely.

"...It's reliable.
Now, let's start by sharing information."

Vermilion Intelligence Agency Headquarters, Strategy Conference Room.

A detailed map of the Crescent region is projected on the hologram display,
Fariel was moving the pointer with a serious expression.

"As a result of analyzing Silver Venom's attack pattern,
We estimated the ``easier areas to attack'' in each country.''

She points out each country one by one, naming them by name.

“First of all, Vermilion.
The influence here is strong, but the military is decentralized and the population is concentrated in urban areas.
The easiest areas to attack are port facilities and commercial districts - just as terrorist bombings have already occurred frequently.
It has a high intimidation effect in places where there are many civilians."

Next is Blue Rose.

“Blue Rose has a lot of industrial areas and abandoned buildings.
Like the abandoned warehouse district where Revilla captured Vivietta-san,
Old industrial areas with little supervision are easy targets.
Our weakness is that there are many places suitable for covert operations.''

Iron Syndicate.

“The military here is strong, but internal factionalism is fierce.
The easiest places to attack are the private residences of upper management and secret meeting facilities.
If individual executives are removed by intimidation, the entire organization will likely collapse.''

Strongest Dominion (SUDOM).

“SUDOM is strong overall, but its remote research facilities are vulnerable.
There are many testing grounds for new weapons and talented people,
If you aim for that, you should be able to aim for technology leakage and talent acquisition at the same time."

Regarding the Stark Empire and the Fatima Federation,
Fariel pointed to the map and accurately listed the weaknesses.

"In conclusion, Silver Venom is not a place with strong military power,"
It appears that they are prioritizing attacks on ``mentally vulnerable areas'' and ``places with symbolic figures.''

Iris folded her arms and nodded silently.

"...That's accurate. Thank you, Fariel."

Fariel blushed a little,
"I'm honored to be praised by Chief Iris!" he said with a small bow.

Next, Miyushari sat down on a chair,
He turned to Iris happily.

“Now then, Chief Iris.
Since I was able to meet you,
Would you like to discuss Silver Venom's "motive" for a moment?

My theory is that they don't just want to dominate;
To “bringing down a strong woman” itself,
I think he has an abnormal obsession.

What do you think?
Is it just a desire for power? Or something more personal...
For example, have you been traumatized by strong women in the past? ”

Iris narrowed her eyes a little,
I answered quietly.

"...I feel the same way.
Looking at Leon and Revilia's actions,
Beyond mere terrorism and desire for control,
There is an almost pathological obsession.
To “destroy” a strong woman,
It looks like you're finding an unusual joy in it.''

Miyushari's eyes sparkled,
I leaned forward.

“Oh yeah!
That's not just a pervert,
“I want to prove my existence by subjugating the strong.”
　Isn't that the flip side of your inferiority complex?
In other words, they know that they are "weak",
They gain a sense of superiority by defeating strong women.
Something like that.”

Elena also listened intently,
He was nodding occasionally.

“Inferiority complex...it certainly makes sense.
That's why we don't kill the victim,
"You're trying to control me mentally."

The discussion became heated;
The three of them delved into Silver Venom's psychology.

Suddenly, Iris interjected.

“By the way...what do you think of Deputy Leader Gareth?
We chased after Levy together, but he was mostly silent...''

Miyushari giggled,
I shrugged.

“Gareth? That guy isn’t that bad.
Although he is quiet, he cares about his friends and is loyal to his duties.
However, I guess I'm the type to keep my distance from women.
There are rumors that something happened in the past...
Well, he's a strong man. Even Bogdus is respected.”

Fariel added in a whisper.

“...Gareth is a person you can trust.
Being able to work together with Director Iris,
　I'm sure you feel honored.''

Iris smiled slightly,
He lightly brushed off his white haori.

“...Yes.
I hope we have a chance to fight together again."

There was a knock on the conference room door.
Three Vermilion government officials came in accompanied by a secretary.

“Excuse me. I heard that you two have arrived from Bogdus Javelin.
　I immediately came for an audience.''

One of the high-ranking officials, an experienced man in charge of foreign affairs, bowed politely.

Miyushari quickly stood up and
He held out his hand brightly.

“Wow, thank you so much!
This is Miyushari. Please join us, Fariel.
Right away, sit down.
I'd like to hear more about Vermilion's current situation.''

The dignitaries took their seats;
We immediately started talking about the threat of Silver Venom.

"We, as a government, consider Silver Venom to be a threat of the highest priority.
Despite the terrorist bombings of the past few days, and the efforts of Director Iris, Leon was captured.
The organization is still alive and well. I'm convinced it's a large-scale conspiracy involving the entire Crescent region."

Miyushari's eyes sparkled,
We immediately started exchanging opinions.

“Oh yeah, that’s it.
Their aim is not just destruction,
To mentally and physically neutralize the symbolic military power of the region.
Because Vermilion has a strong influence,
High-ranking officials and people at the headquarters level are likely to be targeted.
Are you thinking specifically about how to solidify your defense line? ”

The high official nodded seriously and answered.

“We have already evacuated some important people,
We are strengthening cooperation with intelligence agencies.
If necessary, officially consider it a state of war,
"I'm ready for an all-out confrontation."

Fariel also opened her mouth, as if getting involved.

“...A word from me as well.
Those with Silver Venom abilities not only have high individual combat power, but also
They are good at escape and stealth.
The urban area of Vermilion is densely populated and difficult to monitor, so
We recommend strengthening the AI surveillance network and cooperation with the private sector."

Iris joined in, quietly but forcefully.

"I appreciate the government's determination.
We, the intelligence agencies, will do our best to provide information,
Don't miss the opportunity for a pre-emptive strike.
Silver Venom threatens the peace of the entire Crescent.

Those with Silver Venom abilities not only have high individual combat power, but also
They are good at escape and stealth.
The urban area of Vermilion is densely populated and difficult to monitor, so
We recommend strengthening the AI surveillance network and cooperation with the private sector."

Iris joined in, quietly but forcefully.

"I appreciate the government's determination.
We, the intelligence agencies, will do our best to provide information,
Don't miss the opportunity for a pre-emptive strike.
Silver Venom threatens the peace of the entire Crescent.

Vermilion takes the lead.
I will definitely destroy it.”

The dignitaries nodded deeply,
The first high-ranking official spoke on his behalf.

"Director Iris's words are reassuring.
Both members of Bogdus Javelin,
Vermilion will fully cooperate.
Let's eliminate this threat together."

Miyushari smiled,
I slightly clenched my fist.

“Okay, it’s decided!
I like the word "war preparedness."
I'm looking forward to the development where justice wins! ”

In the conference room
The government, intelligence, and the determination of the Bogdus warriors...
Tightly tied.

The counterattack against Silver Venom is
It was about to begin in earnest at the national level.
Somewhere--somewhere in the Crescent region, a deep underground facility.

Several holographic shadows were floating in the dimly lit circular conference room.
Executive members of Silver Venom.
Her face has been darkened and her voice has been modulated.

The leader stands in the center.
Dressed in a black robe, only a cold gaze peeks out from behind the hood.
A person whose gender is difficult to discern, giving off a quiet, intimidating presence.

"Levilia and Leon made a mistake."

The leader's voice was low and emotionless, filling the room.

``Revilia is being chased by Iris and Gareth and is on the verge of failing in her attempt to escape.
Leon was captured by Iris alone.
Both of them damaged the prestige of the organization.
Therefore, I will expel you from Silver Venom.''

One of the projected shadows moved slightly,
No one objected.

The leader continued.

"There's a lot of attention on us right now.
Government, intelligence agencies, Bogdus Javelin...
In particular, the incident near Vermilion is the most frustrating.''

His eyes narrowed slightly behind the hood.

``Iris's performance unexpectedly attracted the attention of the public.
"That woman is more troublesome than I imagined."

The leader slowly raised his hand,

The darkness of Silver Venom is
It began to move deeper and more quietly.

The names of the four people are
It was a moment marked as a target for death.
Above Vermilion, there was a cloudless blue sky.

On the roof of the intelligence agency headquarters, Iris, Miyushari, Fariel, Elena, and the elite members of the Vermilion vigilante group,
A final check of the defense line was being made.

"So much power is coming together.
It would be suicidal for Silver Venom to surprise us.''

Miyushari looked around while making a lighthearted comment.

That moment――

A huge "shadow" appeared in the sky.

Something like a black cloud suddenly covered the sky,
Countless bombs rained down.

Do-do-do-do-do! !

Explosive sounds continued,
A building in the commercial district was engulfed in flames.
A pillar of flame rises at the port facility.

Iris watched from the rooftop,
For the first time, I lost my expression.

“...By no means... from the sky?
"On this scale..."

Elena and the members of the vigilante group,
I was overwhelmed with surprise and despair.

Miyushari immediately narrowed her eyes,
Activated a special "clairvoyance" ability.

“…That’s it! It’s in the sky!
A person is floating in the center of the shadow!
He's the reason why he's dropping bombs! ”

Fariel calmly said,
I raise my hand in a way that distorts the space,
He pulled out a long sniper rifle from the void.

“Distance, about 8 kilometers. No wind.
...I can shoot."

Bang!

A dry gunshot rang out,
The shadows in the sky swayed.

The next moment,
The black shadow collapses,
A mysterious person began to crash.

Fiona is a powerful figure in Fallujah,

There, there was a person wearing a black cloak.
It was smoking and collapsed.

Iris approaches,
When I take off my cloak,
A golden snake emblem shone on its chest.

"...Golden Venom?"

Miyushari muttered with a confused expression.

“Eh, Golden Venom...
A subspecies of Silver Venom? Derived?
Or another organization? ”

Fariel calmly said,
He said while examining the fallen person's equipment.

“…Aren’t you part of a group that’s kind of a joke?
Against Silver Venom,
I was like, ``The golden one is better, right?''
An organization created out of childish rivalry...
I feel like that.”

Miyushari thought for a moment,
I started expressing my personal opinion.

“In my opinion,
Because Silver Venom attracted too much attention,
I think similar criminal organizations or opposing forces may have taken advantage of the situation.
From the name Golden Venom,
It's obvious you're thinking about silver, right?
The appeal that ``we are better'' is clearly visible.
However, flashy attacks like bomb rain,
It's completely different from Silver Venom's cautious style.
　In other words, there is a high possibility that it is a different organization.''

The vigilante leader interjected.

“But the timing is too good.
While Silver Venom is attracting attention,
Attacking Vermilion...
We can't dismiss the possibility of collaboration.''

Iris looked at the face of the fallen person,
He said quietly.

"...I'm conscious.
Let's interrogate.
Who is Golden Venom?
Does it have something to do with Silver Venom...
"I'll make you vomit everything."

The group is
The fallen "Golden Snake" is restrained,
He was taken to headquarters.

The sky of Vermilion is
Calmness returned again, but
A new shadow
I was trying to sneak up on her quietly.

Vermilion intelligence agency headquarters, underground interrogation room.

The Golden Venom man was fixed in a special restraint chair.
His golden cloak had been removed and he was sitting in a black battle uniform.

A scar remains on his forehead from Fariel's sniper bullet,
Blood is still smeared.

Iris and Miyushari are the only ones in the room.
Fariel and Elena were standing on the other side of the observation room, watching over the monitor.

Miyushari sat shallowly on a chair,
Sealing the usual bright smile,
He pierced the man with his sharp eyes.

"Now then, Golden Venom.
That's a nice name. A rip-off of Silver Venom?
Or is it a sense of rivalry?
The reason why they attacked Vermilion by raining bombs from the sky.
It would be helpful if you let me know right away.''

The man curled his lips a little,
I laughed lowly.

“Is it a rip-off? Don’t make me laugh.
We are “gold”. It’s better than silver.”

Miyushari immediately cuts back.

“So, it has nothing to do with Silver Venom?
Same snake motif, similar terrorist methods...
It's too much to be a coincidence though, right? ”

The man shrugged.

"It's a coincidence.
There's no way I'm going to imitate those guys.
"We are a unique organization."

Miyushari thrusts even sharper.

“Then why now?
At a time when Silver Venom is attracting attention,
A large-scale attack on Vermilion.
Piggybacking? Or did someone ask you to do it?
What is the size of your organization? What about the upper management?
What is the funding source? What is the purpose?
...Please answer everything."

The man was silent for a moment, but
Eventually, he answered, looking bothered.

“Size? There are dozens of people.
There are several people in the upper management above the executive team like me.
The funds come from black market arms trading.
Purpose? It's simple.
The world is rotten. Strong people do whatever they want.
"We're just going to destroy it and create an era of gold."

Miyushari pursues further.

“Is there a lewd element similar to Silver Venom?
Things like slime, abilities, etc.”

The man snorted.

“I won’t do such a vulgar imitation.
We will do it fair and square with bombs and guns.
Playing with women is Silver Venom's exclusive right.''

As the interrogation progresses,
The direct connection to Silver Venom is
It gradually faded away.

Observation room.

Fariel calmly took notes while
I whispered to Elena.

"It's a coincidence.
There's no way I'm going to imitate those guys.
"We are a unique organization."

Miyushari thrusts even sharper.

“Then why now?
At a time when Silver Venom is attracting attention,
A large-scale attack on Vermilion.
Piggybacking? Or did someone ask you to do it?
What is the size of your organization? What about the upper management?
What is the funding source? What is the purpose?
...Please answer everything."

The man was silent for a moment, but
Eventually, he answered, looking bothered.

“Size? There are dozens of people.
There are several people in the upper management above the executive team like me.
The funds come from black market arms trading.
Purpose? It's simple.
The world is rotten. Strong people do whatever they want.
"We're just going to destroy it and create an era of gold."

Miyushari pursues further.

“Is there a lewd element similar to Silver Venom?
Things like slime, abilities, etc.”

The man snorted.

“I won’t do such a vulgar imitation.
We will do it fair and square with bombs and guns.
Playing with women is Silver Venom's exclusive right.''

As the interrogation progresses,
The direct connection to Silver Venom is
It gradually faded away.

Observation room.

Fariel calmly took notes while
I whispered to Elena.

A scar remains on his forehead from Fariel's sniper bullet,
Blood is still smeared.

Iris and Miyushari are the only ones in the room.
Fariel and Elena were standing on the other side of the observation room, watching over the monitor.

Miyushari sat shallowly on a chair,
Sealing the usual bright smile,
He pierced the man with his sharp eyes.

"Now then, Golden Venom.
That's a nice name. A rip-off of Silver Venom?
Or is it a sense of rivalry?
The reason why they attacked Vermilion by raining bombs from the sky.
It would be helpful if you let me know right away."

The man curled his lips a little,
I laughed lowly.

“Is it a rip-off? Don’t make me laugh.
We are “gold”. It’s better than silver.”

Miyushari immediately cuts back.

“So, it has nothing to do with Silver Venom?
Same snake motif, similar terrorist methods...
It's too much to be a coincidence though, right? ”

The man shrugged.

"It's a coincidence.
There's no way I'm going to imitate those guys.
"We are a unique organization."

Observation room.

Fariel calmly took notes while
I whispered to Elena.

“…What is Silver Venom?
It seems that the methods and objectives are fundamentally different.
"Golden Venom appears to be just an extremist terrorist organization."

Elena crossed her arms.
He raised an eyebrow.

“But the timing is too good.
As if to disperse Silver Venom's attention...''

Miyushari returns to the interrogation room.
Finally, looking at the man,
I quietly expressed my personal opinion.

"Your organization has nothing to do with Silver Venom...
At least on the surface.

But that's what I think.

Behind Silver Venom,
I thought there might be a larger "parent organization".

Offshoot groups like Golden Venom,
By intentionally creating opposing forces,
Dividing attention and increasing confusion...
There is a possibility that they are using such a strategy.

You may just become pawns without knowing it.''

The man narrowed his eyes for a moment, but
He quickly scoffed.

"That's an interesting delusion.
"But we're just money."

Miyushari smiled,
I stood up.

“Yes.
Then, what is the true identity of that “gold”?
　Let me ask you more details.''

The questioning continued,
The mystery of Golden Venom only deepens.

However, the possibility of the “parent organization” suggested by Miyushari,
On Iris's head,
It cast a new shadow.
Vermilion intelligence agency headquarters, small conference room late at night.

Only the light from the hologram display illuminates the room,
Iris, Miyushari, and Fariel were sitting around the table.
Elena was away due to another emergency.
This was a completely closed discussion space for the three of us.

Miyushari was the first to start.

"Golden Venom's interrogation results,
It's almost certain that it's not directly related to Silver Venom.
But that's not what I'm concerned about.''

She manipulates the hologram with her fingers,
Silver Venom's incident history and Golden Venom's appearance timing are displayed overlappingly.

“This timing is so good.

"They are manipulating multiple subsidiary organizations to amplify the chaos..."

Iris lightly brushed the sleeves of her white haori,
I opened my mouth quietly.

“The parent organization… right?
Both Leon and Revilla,
Although he hinted at the presence of higher-ups, he didn't say anything at all.
It's not just loyalty,
Either you don't really know, or it would be dangerous if you knew.
There's a possibility that the information is being blocked."

Miyushari's eyes sparkled,
I leaned forward.

“Oh yeah!
Silver Venom is a “front organization”.
Behind that, there is a bigger "parent",
Silver, Golden, and other subsidiary organizations.
What about the hypothesis that they are all pawns of their parents?

The parent organization aims to cause chaos in the entire Crescent region.
Using Silver, who destroys the spirit with lewd terrorism,
Use golden to physically destroy with terrorist bombing,
It's spreading the public's attention...
Something like that.”

Fariel calmly added.

“The purpose of the parent organization is to
It's not just control,
It may be the complete collapse of the existing power in the Crescent region.
Targeting strong women is
To reduce the symbolic military power of each nation.
Chief Iris, Fiona, Vivietta-san...
All of us serve as a source of hope and deterrence in our respective regions.”

Iris closed her eyes,
I said after thinking for a while.

“…If a parent organization exists,
Silver Venom's special method of "obscene blackmail" is also
　Not according to parents' instructions,
It may be Silver's own distorted interpretation.
Parents have a broader perspective,
They just want chaos and destruction...
There is a possibility that

Re-verify all information.

The “real enemy” that lies ahead,

The three of us exchanged glances,
A quiet but certain determination,
filled the room.

Deeper into the darkness of Silver Venom,
There is a bigger shadow lurking...
The three of them decided to seriously pursue this possibility.
Vermilion Government Building, a large hall bathed in afternoon sunlight.

Fariel finished the signing ceremony to establish the first joint institution between Bogdus Javelin and Vermilion.
I left the government building quietly.

She has black hair that reaches her shoulders,
With a sincere smile,
Take the elevator down to the ground floor.

"With this, our opposition to Silver Venom will become even stronger..."

With a small sense of satisfaction in my heart,
Fariel went out the front door of the government building.

That moment――

A strange man suddenly approached from the crowd.
He fired a small spray can into Fariel's face.

Push!

A clear, colorless chemical agent is sprayed all over your face.

"...!?"

Fariel immediately covered her eyes.
Severe pain and abnormal reactions attacked my entire body.

My vision became distorted, my skin felt like it was burning,
It becomes difficult to breathe,
My knees give way.

“What… what is this…!?
"Help me..."

Fariel panicked,
I tried to ask for help from passersby, but
I can't make a sound.

The man quickly grabbed Fariel's arm,
He dragged her into an alley amidst the confusion of the crowd.

After a few seconds,
Fariel completely disappeared from the scene.
